// Onscroll into view animation
(function($) {
    $(window).ready(function() {
        const $maskImages = $('.entrance-animate');

        $maskImages.css({
            'opacity' : '1',
            'transform': 'translateY(0)',
            'transition': 'all 1.5s ease-in'
        });
        
        const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
            entries.forEach((entry) => {
                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                    const $target = $(entry.target);
                    $target.css('opacity', '1');
                        
                    $target.css({
                        'transform': 'translateY(102%)'
                    });
                observer.unobserve(entry.target);
                }
            })
        }, {
            threshold: 0.2
        });
        
        $maskImages.each(function() {
            observer.observe(this);
        });
        
    });

	
	$(window).load(function() {
		
		$(window).scroll(function () {
			
			if (window.innerWidth > 1024) {
				
					if ($(this).scrollTop() > $(document).height() - $(window).height() - 800 ) {
						$('#get--in--touch').css('opacity','0');
						$('#get--in--touch').css('visibility','hidden');
					} else {
						$('#get--in--touch').css('opacity','1');
						$('#get--in--touch').css('visibility','visible');
					}
				
			} else {
				
					if ($(this).scrollTop() > 100 && !($(this).scrollTop() > $(document).height() - $(window).height() - 800) ) {
						$('#get--in--touch').css('opacity','1');
						$('#get--in--touch').css('visibility','visible');
					} else if ($(this).scrollTop() > $(document).height() - $(window).height() - 800 ) {
						$('#get--in--touch').css('opacity','0');
						$('#get--in--touch').css('visibility','hidden');
					} else {
						$('#get--in--touch').css('opacity','0');
						$('#get--in--touch').css('visibility','hidden');
					}
				
			}

		});
		
	});
	
	
		// Mega menu Mouseovers
	$(window).load(function() {
	$.each( elementorFrontend.documentsManager.documents, ( id, document ) => {
		if ( document.getModal ) { 
			document.getModal().on( 'show', () => {
			  
				if (window.innerWidth > 1024) {
					
						$('.softwaresolutions--menu').on('mouseover', () => {
								$('.menu--background--1').css('opacity','1');
							});
							$('.softwaresolutions--menu').mouseleave( () => {
								$('.menu--background--1').css('opacity','0');
							});

						$('.content--menu').on('mouseover', () => {
								$('.menu--background--2').css('opacity','1');
							});
							$('.content--menu').mouseleave( () => {
								$('.menu--background--2').css('opacity','0');
							});


						$('.work--menu').on('mouseover', () => {
								$('.menu--background--3').css('opacity','1');
							});
							$('.work--menu').mouseleave( () => {
								$('.menu--background--3').css('opacity','0');
							});


						$('.aboutus--menu').on('mouseover', () => {
								$('.menu--background--4').css('opacity','1');
							});
							$('.aboutus--menu').mouseleave( () => {
								$('.menu--background--4').css('opacity','0');
							});


						$('.insights--menu').on('mouseover', () => {
								$('.menu--background--5').css('opacity','1');
							});
							$('.insights--menu').mouseleave( () => {
								$('.menu--background--5').css('opacity','0');
							});


						$('.careers--menu').on('mouseover', () => {
								$('.menu--background--6').css('opacity','1');
							});
							$('.careers--menu').mouseleave( () => {
								$('.menu--background--6').css('opacity','0');
							});


						$('.getintouch--menu').on('mouseover', () => {
								$('.menu--background--7').css('opacity','1');
							});
							$('.getintouch--menu').mouseleave( () => {
								$('.menu--background--7').css('opacity','0');
							});
